# IMPORTANT: Source Code Access

**Local source files are not present.** Your workspace does not contain source code. You **MUST** use Sourcegraph MCP tools to discover, read, and understand code before making any changes.

**Target Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`
- Use `repo:^github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0$` filter in keyword_search
- Use `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0` as the `repo` parameter for go_to_definition/find_references/read_file


## Required Workflow

1. **Search first** — Use MCP tools to find relevant files and understand existing patterns
2. **Read remotely** — Use `sg_read_file` to read full file contents from Sourcegraph
3. **Edit locally** — Use Edit, Write, and Bash to create or modify files in your working directory
4. **Verify locally** — Run tests with Bash to check your changes

## Tool Selection

| Goal | Tool |
|------|------|
| Exact symbol/string | `sg_keyword_search` |
| Concepts/semantic search | `sg_nls_search` |
| Trace usage/callers | `sg_find_references` |
| See implementation | `sg_go_to_definition` |
| Read full file | `sg_read_file` |
| Browse structure | `sg_list_files` |
| Find repos | `sg_list_repos` |
| Search commits | `sg_commit_search` |
| Track changes | `sg_diff_search` |
| Compare versions | `sg_compare_revisions` |

**Decision logic:**
1. Know the exact symbol? → `sg_keyword_search`
2. Know the concept, not the name? → `sg_nls_search`
3. Need definition of a symbol? → `sg_go_to_definition`
4. Need all callers/references? → `sg_find_references`
5. Need full file content? → `sg_read_file`

## Scoping (Always Do This)

```
repo:^github.com/ORG/REPO$           # Exact repo (preferred)
repo:github.com/ORG/                 # All repos in org
file:.*\.ts$                         # TypeScript only
file:src/api/                        # Specific directory
```

Start narrow. Expand only if results are empty.

## Efficiency Rules

- Chain searches logically: search → read → references → definition
- Don't re-search for the same pattern; use results from prior calls
- Prefer `sg_keyword_search` over `sg_nls_search` when you have exact terms
- Read 2-3 related files before synthesising, rather than one at a time
- Don't read 20+ remote files without writing code — once you understand the pattern, start implementing

## If Stuck

If MCP search returns no results:
1. Broaden the search query (synonyms, partial identifiers)
2. Try `sg_nls_search` for semantic matching
3. Use `sg_list_files` to browse the directory structure
4. Use `sg_list_repos` to verify the repository name

**Sourcegraph Repository:** `github.com/sg-evals/envoy--v1.33.0`

# Task: Implement Custom Header Injection Filter for Envoy

## Objective
Create a new HTTP filter `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection` that injects
configurable headers into requests and/or responses based on route metadata.

## Requirements

1. **Create filter source files**:
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h` — filter class declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc` — filter implementation
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h` — factory declaration
   - `source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc` — factory registration

2. **Filter behavior**:
   - Implements `Http::StreamDecoderFilter` (request path) and `Http::StreamEncoderFilter` (response path)
   - Reads header injection rules from filter config
   - Supports both request and response header injection
   - Follows Envoy's filter lifecycle (decodeHeaders, encodeHeaders)

3. **Create test file**:
   - `test/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter_test.cc`

## Key Reference Files
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.h` — simple header filter pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/filter.cc` — implementation pattern
- `source/extensions/filters/http/header_to_metadata/config.cc` — factory registration
- `source/extensions/filters/http/common/factory_base.h` — factory base class

## Success Criteria
- Filter header file declares class inheriting from StreamDecoderFilter/StreamEncoderFilter
- Filter implementation has decodeHeaders/encodeHeaders methods
- Factory config file registers the filter
- Follows Envoy naming: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection
- Test file exists

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"
#include "source/common/http/utility.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjection {

CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::CustomHeaderInjectionConfig(const ProtoConfig& config) {
  for (const auto& rule : config.headers()) {
    rules_.push_back({rule.header_name(), rule.header_value(), rule.inject_in_request(),
                      rule.inject_in_response()});
  }
}

PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection::PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection(const PerRouteProtoConfig& config) {
  for (const auto& rule : config.headers()) {
    rules_.push_back({rule.header_name(), rule.header_value(), rule.inject_in_request(),
                      rule.inject_in_response()});
  }
}

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,
                                                                    bool) {
  // Get the effective config (global or route-specific)
  const auto* config =
      Http::Utility::resolveMostSpecificPerFilterConfig<CustomHeaderInjectionConfig>(
          decoder_callbacks_);
  if (!config) {
    config = config_.get();
  }

  if (config) {
    injectHeaders(headers, config->rules(), true);
  }

  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
}

✅ **Filter Behavior**
- Implements `Http::StreamDecoderFilter::decodeHeaders()` for request processing
- Implements `Http::StreamEncoderFilter::encodeHeaders()` for response processing
- Injects configurable headers based on rules
- Supports selective injection (request-only, response-only, or both)

✅ **Configuration**
- Proto-based configuration with `HeaderInjectionRule` messages
- Supports both global and per-route configuration via `DualFactoryBase`
- Simple rule structure: header name, value, and injection flags

namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjection {

using ProtoConfig = envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::CustomHeaderInjection;
using PerRouteProtoConfig = envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::CustomHeaderInjectionPerRoute;

/**
 * Configuration for header injection rules
 */
struct HeaderInjectionRule {
  std::string header_name;
  std::string header_value;
  bool inject_in_request;
  bool inject_in_response;
};

/**
 * Filter configuration
 */
class CustomHeaderInjectionConfig : public Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig {
public:
  CustomHeaderInjectionConfig(const ProtoConfig& config);

  const std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule>& rules() const { return rules_; }

private:
  std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule> rules_;
};

using CustomHeaderInjectionConfigSharedPtr = std::shared_ptr<CustomHeaderInjectionConfig>;

/**
 * Per-route filter configuration
 */
class PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection : public Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig {
public:
  PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection(const PerRouteProtoConfig& config);

  const std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule>& rules() const { return rules_; }

private:
  std::vector<HeaderInjectionRule> rules_;
};

2. WRITE /workspace/source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

#include "envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.pb.h"
#include "source/common/http/utility.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjection {

CustomHeaderInjectionConfig::CustomHeaderInjectionConfig(const ProtoConfig& config) {
  for (const auto& rule : config.headers()) {
    rules_.push_back({rule.header_name(), rule.header_value(), rule.inject_in_request(),
                      rule.inject_in_response()});
  }
}

PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection::PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection(const PerRouteProtoConfig& config) {
  for (const auto& rule : config.headers()) {
    rules_.push_back({rule.header_name(), rule.header_value(), rule.inject_in_request(),
                      rule.inject_in_response()});
  }
}

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,
                                                                    bool) {
  // Get the effective config (global or route-specific)
  const auto* config =
      Http::Utility::resolveMostSpecificPerFilterConfig<CustomHeaderInjectionConfig>(
          decoder_callbacks_);
  if (!config) {
    config = config_.get();
  }

  if (config) {
    injectHeaders(headers, config->rules(), true);
  }

  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
}

          encoder_callbac

4. WRITE /workspace/source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.cc
#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/config.h"

#include "source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h"

#include "envoy/registry/registry.h"

namespace Envoy {
namespace Extensions {
namespace HttpFilters {
namespace CustomHeaderInjection {

absl::StatusOr<Http::FilterFactoryCb>
CustomHeaderInjectionFactoryConfig::createFilterFactoryFromProtoTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::CustomHeaderInjection&
        proto_config,
    const std::string&, Common::DualInfo,
    Server::Configuration::ServerFactoryContext&) {
  auto filter_config = std::make_shared<CustomHeaderInjectionConfig>(proto_config);

  return [filter_config](Http::FilterChainFactoryCallbacks& callbacks) -> void {
    callbacks.addStreamFilter(std::make_shared<CustomHeaderInjectionFilter>(filter_config));
  };
}

absl::StatusOr<Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfigConstSharedPtr>
CustomHeaderInjectionFactoryConfig::createRouteSpecificFilterConfigTyped(
    const envoy::extensions::filters::http::custom_header_injection::v3::CustomHeaderInjectionPerRoute&
        proto_config,
    Server::Configuration::ServerFactoryContext&,
    ProtobufMessage::ValidationVisitor&) {
  return std::make_shared<PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection>(proto_config);
}

REGISTER_FACTORY(CustomHeaderInjectionFactoryConfig,
                 Server::Configuration::NamedHttpFilterConfigFactory);

} // namespace CustomHeaderInjection
} // namespace HttpFilters
} // namespace Extensions
} // namespace Envoy

syntax = "proto3";

package envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3;

import "udpa/annotations/status.proto";

option java_package = "io.envoyproxy.envoy.extensions.filters.http.custom_header_injection.v3";
option java_outer_classname = "CustomHeaderInjectionProto";
option java_multiple_files = true;
option go_package = "github.com/envoyproxy/go-control-plane/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3;custom_header_injectionv3";
option (udpa.annotations.file_status).package_version_status = ACTIVE;

// [#protodoc-title: Custom Header Injection filter configuration]
// [#extension: envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection]

message HeaderInjectionRule {
  // The header name to inject
  string header_name = 1;

  // The header value to inject
  string header_value = 2;

  // Whether to inject this header in requests
  bool inject_in_request = 3;

  // Whether to inject this header in responses
  bool inject_in_response = 4;
}

// Per route configuration for the custom header injection filter.
message CustomHeaderInjectionPerRoute {
  repeated HeaderInjectionRule headers = 1;
}

// Configuration for the custom header injection filter.
message CustomHeaderInjection {
  repeated HeaderInjectionRule headers = 1;
}

    inject_in_request: true
    inject_in_response: false

  EXPECT_EQ("custom-value", incoming_headers.get_("x-custom-header"))

Http::FilterHeadersStatus CustomHeaderInjectionFilter::decodeHeaders(Http::RequestHeaderMap& headers,
                                                                    bool) {
  // Get the effective config (global or route-specific)
  const auto* config =
      Http::Utility::resolveMostSpecificPerFilterConfig<CustomHeaderInjectionConfig>(
          decoder_callbacks_);
  if (!config) {
    config = config_.get();
  }

  if (config) {
    injectHeaders(headers, config->rules(), true);
  }

  return Http::FilterHeadersStatus::Continue;
}

12. WRITE /workspace/IMPLEMENTATION_SUMMARY.md
# Custom Header Injection Filter Implementation

## Overview
This document summarizes the implementation of the `envoy.filters.http.custom_header_injection` HTTP filter for Envoy v1.33.0.

## Files Created

### 1. Proto Definition
- **`api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/custom_header_injection.proto`**
  - Defines `HeaderInjectionRule` message with:
    - `header_name`: The name of the header to inject
    - `header_value`: The value to inject
    - `inject_in_request`: Whether to inject in requests
    - `inject_in_response`: Whether to inject in responses
  - Defines `CustomHeaderInjection` for filter configuration
  - Defines `CustomHeaderInjectionPerRoute` for per-route configuration
  - Follows Envoy extension naming convention

- **`api/envoy/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/v3/BUILD`**
  - Bazel build configuration for proto files

### 2. Filter Implementation

#### Header File
- **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.h`**
  - `CustomHeaderInjectionConfig`: Filter configuration class
    - Inherits from `Router::RouteSpecificFilterConfig`
    - Parses and stores header injection rules
  - `PerRouteCustomHeaderInjection`: Per-route configuration class
  - `CustomHeaderInjectionFilter`: Main filter class
    - Inherits from `Http::PassThroughFilter` and `Logger::Loggable`
    - Implements `decodeHeaders()` for request header injection
    - Implements `encodeHeaders()` for response header injection
    - Private `injectHeaders()` helper method

#### Implementation File
- **`source/extensions/filters/http/custom_header_injection/filter.cc`**

  - `decodeHeaders()`: Processes request headers, returns `FilterHeadersStatus::Continue`
